aligncenter size-full"></figure><h3 class="widget-title" style="text-align: center;">|| गणपति स्तोत्रम् ||</h3><div class="textwidget"><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>प्रणम्य शिरसा देवं गौरीपुत्रं विनायकम् ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>भक्तावासं स्मरेन्नित्यमायु:कामार्थसिद्धये ।।१ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>प्रथमं वक्रतुण्डं च एकदन्तं द्वितीयकम् ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>तृतीयं कृष्णपिङ्गगाक्षं गजवक्त्रं चतुर्थकम् ।।२ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>लम्बोदरं पञ्चमं च षष्ठं विकटमेव च ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>सप्तमं विघ्नराजेन्द्रं धूम्रवर्णं तथाष्टमम् ।।३ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>नवमं भालचन्द्रं च दशमं तु विनायकम् ।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>एकादशं गणपतिं द्वादशं तु गजाननम् ।।४ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>द्वादशैतानि नामानि त्रिसंध्यं य: पठेन्नर: ।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>न च विघ्नभयं तस्य सर्वसिद्धिकरं प्रभो ।।५ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>विद्यार्थी लभते विद्यां धनार्थी लभते धनम् ।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>पुत्रार्थी लभते पुत्रान् मोक्षार्थी लभते गतिम् ।।६ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>जपेत् गणपतिस्तोत्रं षड्भिर्मासै: फलं लभेत् ।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>संवत्सरेण सिद्धिं च लभते नात्र संशय: ।।७ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>अष्टभ्यो ब्राह्मणेभ्यश्च लिखित्वा य: समर्पयेत् ।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>तस्य विद्या भवेत्सर्वा गणेशस्य प्रसादत: ।।८ ।।</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>इति श्री नारदपुराणे संकटविनाशनं श्रीगणपतिस्तोत्रं संपूर्णम् ।</strong></p></div><h3 style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;"><a style="color: #ff0000;" data-label="Ganesh Strotra - Sanskrit"><div class="panel-widget-style panel-widget-style-for-16-0-0-0"><h1 style="text-align: center;">गणपती स्तोत्र</h1><div><p style="text-align: center;">साष्टांग नमन हे माझे गौरीपुत्रा विनायका ।<br />भक्तीनें स्मरतो नित्य आयुःकामार्थ साधती ॥ १ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">प्रथम नांव वक्रतुंड दुसरें एकदंत ते ।<br />तिसरे कृष्णपिंगाक्ष चवथे गजवक्र ते ॥ २ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">पांचवे श्रीलंबोदर सहावें विकट नांव ते ।<br />सातवे विघ्नराजेंद्र आठवे धुम्रवर्ण ते ॥ ३ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">नववे श्री भालचंद्र दहावे श्री विनायक ।<br />अकरावे गणपती बारावे श्री गजानन ॥ ४ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">देवनांवे अशी बारा तीन संध्या म्हणे नर ।<br />विघ्नभीती नसे त्याला प्रभो ! तू सर्व सिद्धिदे ॥ ५ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">विद्यार्थ्याला मिळे विद्या धनार्थ्याला मिळे धन ।<br />पुत्रार्थ्याला मिळे पुत्र मोक्षार्थ्याला मिळे गति ॥ ६ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">जपता गणपती स्तोत्र सहा मासांत हे फळ ।<br />एक वर्ष पुर्ण होतां मिळे सिद्धी न संशय ॥ ७ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">नारदांनी रचिलेले झाले संपू्र्ण स्तोत्र हें ।<br />श्रीधराने मराठींत पठण्या अनुवादिले ॥ ८ ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">॥ श्रीगणपती स्तोत्र संपूर्ण ॥</p><h3 style="text-align: right;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;"><a style="color: #ff0000;" href="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Marathi-2.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Ganesh Stora in Marathi</a></span></strong></h3></div></div></div></div></div></div> aligncenter size-full"></figure><h3 style="text-align: center;">|| Ganapati Stotra || </h3><p style="text-align: center;">Pranamya shirasa devam Gauri vinayakam Bhaktavasam smare nityam ayuh kamartha siddhaye ||1||</p><p style="text-align: center;">Prathamam vakratundam cha ekadantam dvitiyakam Tritiyam krishnapingaksham, gajavaktram chaturthakam ||2||</p><p style="text-align: center;">Lambodaram panchamam cha shashtam Vikatameva cha Saptamam Vighnarajendraṃ, Dhoomravarnam tathaashtamam ||3||</p><p style="text-align: center;">Navamam Bhalachandram cha dashamam tu Vinayakam Ekadasham ganapatim, dvadasham tu gajananam ||4||</p><p style="text-align: center;">Dvadashaitani namani trisandhyam yah pathen naraha Na cha vighna bhayam tasya sarvasiddhi karam prabho ||5||</p><p style="text-align: center;">Vidyarthi labhate vidyam, dhanarthi labhate dhanam Putrarthi labhate putran, mo ksharthi labhate gatim ||6||</p><p style="text-align: center;">Japed Ganapati Stotram shadbhir masaihi phalam labhet Samvatsaren Siddhim cha labhate natra sanshayah ||7||</p><p style="text-align: center;">Ashtabhyo brahmanebhyashcha likhitva yah samarpayet Tasya vidya bhavet sarva ganeshasya prasadatah ||8||</p><p style="text-align: center;">|| Iti Shri Narada Purane Sankshipta Nashana Nam Shri Ganapati Stotram Sampurnam ||</p><h3 style="text-align: right;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;"><a style="color: #ff0000;" href="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/GS_English-1.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Ganesh Stora in English</a></span></strong></h3> aligncenter size-full"></figure><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>|| ગણપતિ સ્તોત્રમ્ || </strong></p><p style="text-align: center;">પ્રણમ્ય શિરસા દેવં ગૌરીપુત્રં વિનાયકમ્ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">ભક્તાવાસં સ્મરેન્નિત્યમાયુ:કામાર્થસિદ્ધયે ।।૧ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">પ્રથમં વક્રતુણ્ડં ચ એકદન્તં દ્વિતીયકમ્ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">તૃતીયં કૃષ્ણપિઙ્ગગાક્ષં ગજવક્ત્રં ચતુર્થકમ્ ।।૨ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">લમ્બોદરં પઞ્ચમં ચ ષષ્ઠં વિકટમેવ ચ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">સપ્તમં વિઘ્નરાજેન્દ્રં ધૂમ્રવર્ણં તથાષ્ટમમ્ ।।૩ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">નવમં ભાલચન્દ્રં ચ દશમં તુ વિનાયકમ્ ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">એકાદશં ગણપતિં દ્વાદશં તુ ગજાનનમ્ ।।૪ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">દ્વાદશૈતાનિ નામાનિ ત્રિસંધ્યં ય: પઠેન્નર: ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">ન ચ વિઘ્નભયં તસ્ય સર્વસિદ્ધિકરં પ્રભો ।।૫ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">વિદ્યાર્થી લભતે વિદ્યાં ધનાર્થી લભતે ધનમ્ ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">પુત્રાર્થી લભતે પુત્રાન્ મોક્ષાર્થી લભતે ગતિમ્ ।।૬ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">જપેત્ ગણપતિસ્તોત્રં ષડ્ભિર્માસૈ: ફલં લભેત્ ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">સંવત્સરેણ સિદ્ધિં ચ લભતે નાત્ર સંશય: ।।૭ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">અષ્ટભ્યો બ્રાહ્મણેભ્યશ્ચ લિખિત્વા ય: સમર્પયેત્ ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">તસ્ય વિદ્યા ભવેત્સર્વા ગણેશસ્ય</p><p style="text-align: center;">પ્રસાદત: ।।૮ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">ઇતિ શ્રી નારદપુરાણે સંકટવિનાશનં શ્રીગણપતિસ્તોત્રં સંપૂર્ણમ્ ।</p><h3 style="text-align: aligncenter size-full"></figure><h2 style="text-align: center;">|| గణపతి స్తోత్రం ||</h2><p style="text-align: center;">ప్రణమ్య శిరసా దేవం గౌరీ వినాయకం । భక్తావాసం స్మేర నిత్యమాయ్ః కామార్థసిద్ధయే ॥१॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ప్రథమం వక్రతుడం చ ఏకదంత ద్వితీయకమ్ । తృతియం కృష్ణపింగాత్క్షం గజవవత్రం చతుర్థకమ్ ॥२॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">లంబోదరం పంచమ చ పష్ఠం వికటమేవ చ । సప్తమం విఘ్నరాజేంద్రం ధూమ్రవర్ణ తథాష్టమమ్ ॥३॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">నవమం భాలచంద్రం చ దశమం తు వినాయకమ్ । ఏకాదశం గణపతిం ద్వాదశం తు గజానన్ ॥४॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ద్వాదశైతాని నామాని త్రిసంఘ్యంయః పఠేన్నరః । న చ విఘ్నభయం తస్య సర్వసిద్ధికరం ప్రభో ॥५॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">విద్యార్థీ లభతే విద్యాం, ధనార్థీ లభతే ధనం, పుత్రార్థీ లభతే పుత్రాన్, మోక్షార్థీ లభతే గతిం॥6॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">జపేద్గణపతి స్తోత్రం షడిభిర్మాసైః ఫలం లభతే, సంవత్సరేణ సిద్ధించ లభతే నాత్ర సంశయః॥7॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">అష్టభ్యో బ్రాహ్మణేభ్యః శ్రుత్వా ఫలం లభతే, తస్య విద్యా భవేత్సర్వా గణేశస్య ప్రసాదతః॥8॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ఇది శ్రీ నారద పురాణంలో సంకష్టనాశనం నామ శ్రీ గణపతి స్తోత్రం సంపూర్ణం॥</p><h3 style="text-align: right;"><strong><span style="color: aligncenter size-full"></figure><h3 style="text-align: center;">|| கணபதி ஸ்தோத்ரம் ||</h3><p style="text-align: center;">பிரணம்ய சிரஸா தேவம் கௌரி விநாயகம்,<br />பக்தவாஸம் ஸ்மேர் நித்யமாய் காமார்த்த சித்தயே. ॥ 1 ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">முதல் வக்ரதுண்டம் மற்றும் இரண்டாம் ஏகதந்தம் மூன்றாம் கருணைபிங்காட்சம் நான்காம் கமலவத்திரம் ஆகியவற்றை மணித்துவதற்கு வழிகாட்டியது. ॥ 2 ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">லம்போதரம் பஞ்சமம் ச பஷ்டம் விகடமேவ ச । ஸப்தமம் விக்னராஜேந்த்ரம் தூம்ரவர்ண ததாஷ்டமம் ॥3॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">நவமம் பாலசந்திரம் ச தசமம் து விநாயகம், ஏகாதசம் கணபதிம் த்வாதசம் து கஜானன் ॥४॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">த்வாதஶைதானி நாமானி த்ரிஸங்க்யஂயஃ ப஠ேந்னரஃ । ந ச விக்நபயம் தஸ்ய ஸர்வஸித்திகரம் ப்ரபோ ॥ 5 ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">வித்யார்தி லபதே வித்யாம் தனார்தி லபதே தனம்। புத்ரார்தி லபதே புத்ரான் மோக்ஷார்தி லபதே கதிம்॥ 6 ॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ஜபேத் நபதிஸ்தோத்ரம் ஷடிபர்மாஸைஃ பலம் லபதே । ஸம்வத்ஸரேண சித்திம்ச லபதே நாத்ர ஸஞ்சயஃ ॥7॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">அஷ்டப்பிரஹ्मணேப்யஃ ஸ்ரச்த்வா லிக்கித்வா பலம் லபதே। தஸ்ய வித்யா பவேத்ஸர்வா கணேஷஸ்ய ப்ரஸாததஃ॥ 8॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">இது ஶ்ரீ நாரத புராணத்தில் உள்ள ஸங்கடநாசனம் என்ற பெயருடைய ஸ்ரீ கணபதி ஸ்தோத்ரம் முழுவதும் இதுவரையும் முடிந்துள்ளது॥</p><h3 style="text-align: right;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;"><a style="color: #ff0000;" href="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/GS_Tamil.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Ganesh Stora in Tamil</a></span></strong></h3>                        </div>

https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1.jpg 512w" sizes="(max-width: 127px) 100vw, 127px" /></p></figure><figure></figure><figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"></figure><p><span class="Y2IQFc" lang="ml">|| ഗണപതി സ്തോത്രം ||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">പ്രണമ്യ ശിരസാ ദേവം ഗൗരീ വിനായകം ഭക്താവാസം സ്മേര നിത്യമായ് കാമാർത്ഥസിദ്ധയേ ॥1॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">പ്രഥമം വക്രതുഡം ച ഏകദംത ദ്വിതീയകം തൃതിയം കൃഷ്ണപിംഗാത്ക്ഷം ഗജവവത്രം ചതുർത്ഥകം ॥2॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ലംബോദരം പഞ്ചമം ച പഷ്ഠം വികടമേവ ച സപ്തമം വിഘ്നരാജേന്ദ്രം ധൂമ്രവർണ തഥാഷ്ടമമ് ॥3॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">നവം ഭാലചന്ദ്രം ച ദശമം തു വിനായകം ഏകാദശം ഗണപതിം ദ്വാദശം തു ഗജാനന് ॥4॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ദ്വാദശൈതാനി നാമാനി ത്രിസംഘ്യംയഃ പഠേൻനരഃ ന ച വിഘ്നഭയം തസ്യ സര്‍വസിദ്ധികരം പ്രഭോ ॥5॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">വിദ്യാര്‍ത്ഥി ലഭതേ വിദ്യാം ധനാര്‍ത്ഥി ലഭതേ ധനം പുത്രാര്‍ത്ഥി ലഭതേ പുത്രാന്മോക്ഷാര്‍ത്ഥി ലഭതേ ഗതിം ॥6॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ജപേദ്ഗണപതിസ്തോത്രം ഷഡിഭൈര്‍മാസൈഃ ഫലം ലഭതേ സംവത്സരേണ സിദ്ധിംച ലഭതേ നത്ര സംശയഃ ॥7॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">അഷ്ടഭ്യോ ബ്രാഹ്മണേഭ്യശ്ച ലിഖിത്വാ ഫലം ലഭതേ തസ്യ വിദ്യാ ഭവേത്സര്‍വാ ഗണേശസ്യ പ്രസാദതഃ ॥8॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ഇതി ശ്രീ നാരദ പുരാണേ സംകഷ്ടനാശനം നാമ ശ്രീഗണപതി സ്തോത്രം സംപൂര്‍ണ്ണം</p><h3 style="text-align: right;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;"><a style="color: #ff0000;" href="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/GS_Malayalam.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Ganesh Stora in Malayalam</a></span></strong></h3>                        </div>

কামাৰ্থসিদ্ধয়ে ॥১॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">প্ৰথমং বক্ৰতুডং চ একদংত দ্বিতীয়কম্‌। তৃতীয়ং কৃষ্ণপিংগাত্ক্ষং গজববত্ৰং চতুৰ্থকম্‌ ॥২॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">লম্বোদৰং পঞ্চম চ পষ্ঠং বিকটমেব চ। সপ্তমং বিঘ্নৰাজেংদ্ৰং ধূম্ৰবৰ্ণ তথাষ্টমম্‌ ॥৩॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">নবমং ভালচন্দ্ৰং চ দশমং তু বিনায়কম্‌। একাদশং গণপতিং দ্বাদশং তু গজানন্‌ ॥৪॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">দ্বাদশৈতানি নামানি ত্ৰিসংঘ্যংয়ঃ পঠেন্নৰঃ। ন চ বিঘ্নভয়ং তস্য সৰ্বসিদ্ধিকৰং প্ৰভো ॥৫॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ভিদ্যার্থী লভতে বিদ্যাং ধনার্থী লভতে ধনম্ । পুত্রার্থী লভতে পুত্রান্মো ক্ষার্থী লভতে গতিং ॥৬॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">জপেদ্ণপতি স্তোত্রং ষডিভর্মাসৈঃ ফলং লভতে । সংবত্সরেণ সিদ্ধিংচ লভতে নাত্র সংশয়ঃ ॥৭॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">অষ্টভ্যো ব্রাহ্মণে ভ্যশ্র্চ লিখিত্বা ফলং লভতে । তস্য বিদ্যা ভবেত্সর্বা গণেশস্য প্রসাদতঃ ॥৮॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">॥ ইতি শ্রী নারদ পুরাণে সংকষ্টনাশনং নাম শ্রী গণপতি স্তোত্রং সংপূর্ণম্ ॥</p><h3 style="text-align: style="text-align: center;">ਪਹਿਲਾਂ ਵਕਰ ਤੁੰਡ ਚ ਦੂਜਾ ਏਕਦੰਤ ਹੈ । ਤੀਜਾ ਕਲਾਂਤ ਸਿਆਹ ਰੰਗ ਦਾ ਚੌਥਾ ਹੈ ਹਾਥ ਵਾਲਾ ॥੨॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ਪੰਜਵੇਂ ਲੰਬੋਦਰ ਹੈ ਛੇਵੇਂ ਭਯੰਕਰ ਹੈ । ਸਤਵੇਂ ਵਿਘਨਰਾਜ ਇੰਦਰ ਹੈ ਅਠਵੇਂ ਧੂਮਵਰਣ ਹੈ ॥੩॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ਨਵੇਂ ਭਾਲਚੰਦਰ ਹੈ ਦਸਵੇਂ ਵਿਨਾਯਕ ਹੈ । ਇਕਾਦਸਵੇਂ ਗਣਪਤੀ ਹੈ ਦੋਧਵੇਂ ਵਿਨਾਯਕ ਹੈ ॥੪॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ਇਹ ਗਿਣਤੀ ਨਾਮ ਹੈਂ ਤੇ ਤਿੰਨ ਦੁਹਾਈ ਦੇਣਾ ਹੈ । ਪੜਨ ਵਾਲੇ ਦਾ ਕੋਈ ਭੀ ਕਿਸੇ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ ਦਾ ਭਯ ਨਹੀਂ ਹੁੰਦਾ ਹੈ। ॥੫॥</p><div class="group w-full text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-100 border-b border-black/10 dark:border-gray-900/50 bg-gray-50 aligncenter size-full"></figure><h2 style="text-align: center;"><strong>|| গণপতি স্তোত্র ||</strong></h2><p style="text-align: center;">প্রণম্য শিরসা দেবং গৌরী বিনায়কম্ । ভক্তাবাসং স্মের নিত্যমায়ঃ কামার্থসিদ্ধয়ে ॥১॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">প্রথমং বক্রতুডং চ একদংত দ্বিতীয়কম্ । তৃতিয়ং কৃষ্ণপিংগাত্ক্ষং গজববত্রং চতুর্থকম্ ॥২॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">লম্বোদরং পঞ্চম চ পষ্ঠং বিকটমেব চ । সপ্তমং বিঘ্নরাজেংদ্রং ধূম্রবর্ণ তথাষ্টমম্ ॥৩॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">নবমং ভালচংদ্রং চ দশমং তু বিনায়কম্ । একাদশং গণপতিং দ্বাদশং তু গজানন্ ॥৪॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">দ্বাদশএতানি নামানি ত্রিসংঘ্যংযঃ পঠেন্নরঃ । ন চ বিঘ্নভয়ং তস্য সর্বসিদ্ধিকরং প্রভো ॥৫॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">বাংলায় লিখতে হলে এইভাবে লিখতে হবেঃ</p><p style="text-align: center;">বিদ্যার্থী লভতে বিদ্যাং ধনার্থী লভতে ধনম্ । পুত্রার্থী লভতে পুত্রান্ মো ক্ষার্তী লভতে গতিম্ ॥৬॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">জপেদ্ব পতিস্তোত্রং ষডিভর্মাসৈঃ ফলং লভতে । সংবত্সরেণ সিদ্ধিংচ লভতে নাত্র সংশয়ঃ ॥৭॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">অষ্টভ্যো ব্রাহ্মণে ভ্যশ্র্চ লিখিত্বা ফলং লভতে । তস্য বিদ্যা ভবেত্সর্বা গণেশস্য প্রসাদতঃ ॥৮॥</p><p style="text-align: center;">ইতি শ্রী নারদ পুরাণে সংকষ্টনাশনং নাম শ্রী গণপতি স্তোত্রং সংপূর্ণম্ ॥</p><h3 style="text-align: right;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;"><a style="color: #ff0000;" href="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/GS_bengali.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Ganesh Stora in Bengali</a></span></strong></h3>                        </div>
                    </div>

                        <div class="animated fadeIn">
                            <figure><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-1354 aligncenter" src="http://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-300x300.jpg" alt="Ganpati stotra meaning in English with Sanskrit lyrics" width="127" height="127" 32w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/elementor/thumbs/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-q6u8uygyeyt76ohz5jof9fabh1yftv1d84y6tcmees.jpg 50w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/elementor/thumbs/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-q6u8uygywibrtvrgx40w3utnvzn3akbnkus99wtaf8.jpg 90w, aligncenter size-full"></figure><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">|| <strong>ಗಣಪತಿ ಸ್ತೋತ್ರ</strong> ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ಪ್ರಣಮ್ಯ ಶಿರಸಾ ದೇವಂ ಗೌರೀಪುತ್ರಂ ವಿನಾಯಕಂ |<br />ಭಕ್ತಾವಾಸಂ ಸ್ಮರೇನ್ನಿತ್ಯಂ ಆಯುಃ ಕಾಮಾರ್ಥ ಸಿದ್ಧಯೆ || ೧ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ಪ್ರಥಮಂ ವಕ್ರತುಂಡಂ ಚ ಏಕದಂತಂ ದ್ವಿತೀಯಕಂ|<br />ತೃತೀಯಂ ಕೃಷ್ಣಪಿಂಗಾಕ್ಷಂ ಗಜವಕ್ತ್ರಂ ಚತುರ್ಥಕಂ|| ೨ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ಲಂಬೋದರಂ ಪಂಚಮಂ ಚ ಷಷ್ಠಂ ವಿಕಟಮೇವ ಚ |<br />ಸಪ್ತಮಂ ವಿಘ್ನರಾಜೇಂದ್ರಂ ಧೂಮ್ರವರ್ಣಂ ತಥಾಷ್ಟಮಂ || ೩ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ನವಮಂ ಭಾಲಚಂದ್ರಂ ಚ ದಶಮಂ ತು ವಿನಾಯಕಂ|<br />ಏಕಾದಶಂ ಗಣಪತಿಂ ದ್ವಾದಶಂ ತು ಗಜಾನನಂ|| ೪ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ದ್ವಾದಶೈತಾನಿ ನಾಮಾನಿ ತ್ರಿಸಂಧ್ಯಂ ಯಃ ಪಠೇನ್ನರಃ |<br />ನ ಚ ವಿಘ್ನಭಯಂ ತಸ್ಯ ಸರ್ವಸಿದ್ಧಿಕರಂ ಪ್ರಭೋ || ೫ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ವಿದ್ಯಾರ್ಥಿ ಲಭತೆ ವಿದ್ಯಾಂ ಧನಾರ್ಥೀ ಲಭತೆ ಧನಂ |<br />ಪುತ್ರಾರ್ಥಿ ಲಭತೆ ಪುತ್ರಾನ್ ಮೋಕ್ಷಾರ್ಥಿ ಲಭತೆ ಗತಿಂ|| ೬ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ಜಪೇತ್ ಗಣಪತಿಸ್ತೋತ್ರಂ ಷಡ್ಭಿರ್ಮಾಸೈಃ ಫಲಂ ಲಭೇತ್ |<br />ಸಂವತ್ಸರೇಣ ಸಿದ್ಧಿಂ ಚ ಲಭತೆ ನಾತ್ರ ಸಂಶಯಃ || ೭ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ಅಷ್ಟೆಭ್ಯೊ ಬ್ರಾಹ್ಮಣೇಭ್ಯಶ್ಚ ಲಿಖಿತ್ವಾ ಯಃ ಸಮರ್ಪಯೇತ್ |<br />ತಸ್ಯ ವಿದ್ಯಾ ಭವೇತ್ ಸರ್ವಾ ಗಣೇಶಸ್ಯ ಪ್ರಸಾದತಃ || ೮ ||</p><p class="has-text-align-center" style="text-align: center;">ಇತಿ ಶ್ರೀ ನಾರದ ಪುರಾಣೇ ಸಂಕಷ್ಟನಾಶನಂ ನಾಮ ಶ್ರೀ ಗಣಪತಿ ಸ್ತೋತ್ರಂ ಸಂಪೂರ್ಣಮ್.</p><h3 style="text-align: right;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;"><a style="color: #ff0000;" href="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/GS_kannada.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Ganesh Stora in Kannada</a></span></strong></h3>                        </div>

                                    <div class="tab-pane elementkit-tab-pane elementor-repeater-item-0c0cc5a " id="content-0c0cc5a699cbf97da0ca" role="tabpanel"
                         aria-labelledby="content-0c0cc5a699cbf97da0ca-tab">
                        <div class="animated fadeIn">
                            <figure><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-1354 aligncenter" src="http://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-300x300.jpg" alt="Ganpati stotra meaning in English with Sanskrit lyrics" width="127" height="127" srcset="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-300x300.jpg 300w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-270x270.jpg 270w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-192x192.jpg 192w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-32x32.jpg 32w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/elementor/thumbs/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-q6u8uygyeyt76ohz5jof9fabh1yftv1d84y6tcmees.jpg 50w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1.jpg 512w" sizes="(max-width: 127px) 100vw, 127px" /></p></figure><figure></figure><figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"></figure><p style="text-align: center;">|| गणपति स्तोत्रम् ||</p><div id="pl-16" class="panel-layout"><div id="pg-16-0" class="panel-grid panel-no-style"><div id="pgc-16-0-0" class="panel-grid-cell" data-weight="1"><div id="panel-16-0-0-0" class="so-panel widget widget_text panel-first-child panel-last-child" data-index="0" data-style="{&quot;background_image_attachment&quot;:false,&quot;background_display&quot;:&quot;tile&quot;,&quot;background_image_size&quot;:&quot;full&quot;,&quot;border_thickness&quot;:&quot;1px&quot;,&quot;box_shadow&quot;:&quot;on&quot;,&quot;box_shadow_color&quot;:&quot;rgba(0,0,0,0.15)&quot;,&quot;box_shadow_inset&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;box_shadow_offset_horizontal&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;box_shadow_offset_vertical&quot;:&quot;5px&quot;,&quot;box_shadow_blur&quot;:&quot;15px&quot;}" data-label="Ganesh Strotra - Sanskrit"><div class="panel-widget-style panel-widget-style-for-16-0-0-0"><div class="textwidget"><p style="text-align: center;">नारद उवाच </p><p style="text-align: center;">Narada Uvacha:</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">Sage Narada told</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">प्रणम्य शिरसा देवं गौरीपुत्रं विनायकम् ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">भक्तावासं स्मरेन्नित्यमायु:कामार्थसिद्धये ।।१ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">The one seeking longevity, wealth, and love, Should bow their head in reverence To Lord Ganapathi, the son of Goddess Parvathi, Who is the embodiment of wisdom and grace ||1||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">प्रथमं वक्रतुण्डं च एकदन्तं द्वितीयकम् ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">तृतीयं कृष्णपिङ्गगाक्षं गजवक्त्रं चतुर्थकम् ।।२ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">First, perceive him as the deity with a broken tusk, Second, envision him as the Lord with a single tusk, Third, recognize him as the one with eyes of reddish-black hue, Fourth, behold him as the divine being with an elephant-like face.||2||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">लम्बोदरं पञ्चमं च षष्ठं विकटमेव च ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;">सप्तमं विघ्नराजेन्द्रं धूम्रवर्णं तथाष्टमम् ।।३ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">Fifth, behold him with a broad and ample belly, Sixth, recognize him as the fierce adversary of his foes, Seventh, revere him as the remover of all obstacles, Eighth, perceive him with a complexion akin to the hue of smoke||3||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">नवमं भालचन्द्रं च दशमं तु विनायकम् ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">एकादशं गणपतिं द्वादशं तु गजाननम् ।।४ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">Ninth, acknowledge him with the crescent adorning his forehead, Tenth, honor him as the supreme leader in removing obstacles, Eleventh, revere him as the commander of Lord Shiva&#8217;s celestial army, And twelfth, behold him with the majestic countenance of an elephant ||4||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">द्वादशैतानि नामानि त्रिसंध्यं य: पठेन्नर: ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">न च विघ्नभयं तस्य सर्वसिद्धिकरं प्रभो ।।५ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">Anyone who recites these twelve names, At dawn, noon, and dusk, Shall never fear defeat, And shall always attain their desired goals.||5||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">विद्यार्थी लभते विद्यां धनार्थी लभते धनम् ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">पुत्रार्थी लभते पुत्रान् मोक्षार्थी लभते गतिम् ।।६ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">The seeker of knowledge shall attain wisdom, The seeker of wealth shall attain abundance, The one desiring a son shall be blessed with a child, And the one seeking salvation shall attain liberation.||6||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">जपेत् गणपतिस्तोत्रं षड्भिर्मासै: फलं लभेत् ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">संवत्सरेण सिद्धिं च लभते नात्र संशय: ।।७ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">The fruits of chanting this prayer, To Lord Ganapati, shall manifest in six months, And within a year, all desires shall be fulfilled, With no doubt remaining, this truth stands affirmed.||7||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">अष्टभ्यो ब्राह्मणेभ्यश्च लिखित्वा य: समर्पयेत् ।</p><p style="text-align: center;">तस्य विद्या भवेत्सर्वा गणेशस्य प्रसादत: ।।८ ।।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">The one who shares this prayer, In writing, with eight wise beings, And presents it as an offering to Lord Ganesha, Shall be bestowed with wisdom, And blessed with virtues by the grace of Lord Ganesha.||8||</span></p><p style="text-align: center;">इति श्री नारदपुराणे संकटविनाशनं श्रीगणपतिस्तोत्रं संपूर्णम् ।</p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;">Thus concludes the sacred prayer from the Narada Purana to Lord Ganesha, Which has the power to dispel all sorrows and afflictions.</span></p><p style="text-align: center;"> </p></div></div></div></div></div></div>                        </div>
                    </div>
                                    <div class="tab-pane elementkit-tab-pane elementor-repeater-item-7ea4e07 " id="content-7ea4e07699cbf97da0ca" role="tabpanel"
                         aria-labelledby="content-7ea4e07699cbf97da0ca-tab">
                        <div class="animated fadeIn">
                            <figure><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-1354 aligncenter" src="http://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-300x300.jpg" alt="Ganpati stotra meaning in English with Sanskrit lyrics" width="127" height="127" srcset="https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-300x300.jpg 300w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-150x150.jpg 150w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-270x270.jpg 270w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-192x192.jpg 192w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-32x32.jpg 32w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/elementor/thumbs/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-q6u8uygyeyt76ohz5jof9fabh1yftv1d84y6tcmees.jpg 50w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/elementor/thumbs/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-q6u8uygywibrtvrgx40w3utnvzn3akbnkus99wtaf8.jpg 90w, https://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1.jpg 512w" sizes="(max-width: 127px) 100vw, 127px" /></p></figure><figure></figure><figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"></figure><div class="textwidget"><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>|| Ganapati Stotra || </strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Narada Uvacha:</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>Sage Narada told</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Pranamya shirasa devam Gauri vinayakam Bhaktavasam smare nityam ayuh kamartha siddhaye ||1||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>The one seeking longevity, wealth, and love, Should bow their head in reverence To Lord Ganapathi, the son of Goddess Parvathi, Who is the embodiment of wisdom and grace ||1||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Prathamam vakratundam cha ekadantam dvitiyakam Tritiyam krishnapingaksham, gajavaktram chaturthakam ||2||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>First, perceive him as the deity with a broken tusk, Second, envision him as the Lord with a single tusk, Third, recognize him as the one with eyes of reddish-black hue, Fourth, behold him as the divine being with an elephant-like face.||2||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Lambodaram panchamam cha shashtam Vikatameva cha Saptamam Vighnarajendraṃ, Dhoomravarnam tathaashtamam ||3||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>Fifth, behold him with a broad and ample belly, Sixth, recognize him as the fierce adversary of his foes, Seventh, revere him as the remover of all obstacles, Eighth, perceive him with a complexion akin to the hue of smoke||3||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Navamam Bhalachandram cha dashamam tu Vinayakam Ekadasham ganapatim, dvadasham tu gajananam ||4||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>Ninth, acknowledge him with the crescent adorning his forehead, Tenth, honor him as the supreme leader in removing obstacles, Eleventh, revere him as the commander of Lord Shiva&#8217;s celestial army, And twelfth, behold him with the majestic countenance of an elephant ||4||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Dvadashaitani namani trisandhyam yah pathen naraha Na cha vighna bhayam tasya sarvasiddhi karam prabho ||5||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>Anyone who recites these twelve names, At dawn, noon, and dusk, Shall never fear defeat, And shall always attain their desired goals.||5||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Vidyarthi labhate vidyam, dhanarthi labhate dhanam Putrarthi labhate putran, mo ksharthi labhate gatim ||6||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>The seeker of knowledge shall attain wisdom, The seeker of wealth shall attain abundance, The one desiring a son shall be blessed with a child, And the one seeking salvation shall attain liberation.||6||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Japed Ganapati Stotram shadbhir masaihi phalam labhet Samvatsaren Siddhim cha labhate natra sanshayah ||7||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>The fruits of chanting this prayer, To Lord Ganapati, shall manifest in six months, And within a year, all desires shall be fulfilled, With no doubt remaining, this truth stands affirmed.||7||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Ashtabhyo brahmanebhyashcha likhitva yah samarpayet Tasya vidya bhavet sarva ganeshasya prasadatah ||8||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>The one who shares this prayer, In writing, with eight wise beings, And presents it as an offering to Lord Ganesha, Shall be bestowed with wisdom, And blessed with virtues by the grace of Lord Ganesha.||8||</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong> Iti Shri Narada Purane Sankshipta Nashana Nam Shri Ganapati Stotram Sampurnam ||</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #800000;"><strong>Thus concludes the sacred prayer from the Narada Purana to Lord Ganesha, Which has the power to dispel all sorrows and afflictions.</strong></span></p></div>                        </div>

/></p></figure><figure></figure><figure class=\"wp-block-image aligncenter size-full\"></figure><h3>|| Ganapati Stotra || </h3><p>Pranamya shirasa devam Gauri vinayakam Bhaktavasam smare nityam ayuh kamartha siddhaye ||1||</p><p>Prathamam vakratundam cha ekadantam dvitiyakam Tritiyam krishnapingaksham, gajavaktram chaturthakam ||2||</p><p>Lambodaram panchamam cha shashtam Vikatameva cha Saptamam Vighnarajendraṃ, Dhoomravarnam tathaashtamam ||3||</p><p>Navamam Bhalachandram cha dashamam tu Vinayakam Ekadasham ganapatim, dvadasham tu gajananam ||4||</p><p>Dvadashaitani namani trisandhyam yah pathen naraha Na cha vighna bhayam tasya sarvasiddhi karam prabho ||5||</p><p>Vidyarthi labhate vidyam, dhanarthi labhate dhanam Putrarthi labhate putran, mo ksharthi labhate gatim ||6||</p><p>Japed Ganapati Stotram shadbhir masaihi phalam labhet Samvatsaren Siddhim cha labhate natra sanshayah ||7||</p><p>Ashtabhyo brahmanebhyashcha likhitva yah samarpayet Tasya vidya bhavet sarva ganeshasya prasadatah ||8||</p><p>|| Iti Shri Narada Purane Sankshipta Nashana Nam Shri Ganapati Stotram Sampurnam ||</p><h3><strong><span style=\"color: #ff0000\"><a style=\"color: #ff0000\" ।</p><p>ન ચ વિઘ્નભયં તસ્ય સર્વસિદ્ધિકરં પ્રભો ।।૫ ।।</p><p>વિદ્યાર્થી લભતે વિદ્યાં ધનાર્થી લભતે ધનમ્ ।</p><p>પુત્રાર્થી લભતે પુત્રાન્ મોક્ષાર્થી લભતે ગતિમ્ ।।૬ ।।</p><p>જપેત્ ગણપતિસ્તોત્રં ದ್ವಿತೀಯಕಂ|<br />ತೃತೀಯಂ ಕೃಷ್ಣಪಿಂಗಾಕ್ಷಂ ಗಜವಕ್ತ್ರಂ ಚತುರ್ಥಕಂ|| ೨ ||</p><p class=\"has-text-align-center\">ಲಂಬೋದರಂ ಪಂಚಮಂ ಚ ಷಷ್ಠಂ ವಿಕಟಮೇವ ಚ |<br />ಸಪ್ತಮಂ ವಿಘ್ನರಾಜೇಂದ್ರಂ ಧೂಮ್ರವರ್ಣಂ ತಥಾಷ್ಟಮಂ || ೩ ||</p><p class=\"has-text-align-center\">ನವಮಂ ಭಾಲಚಂದ್ರಂ ಚ ದಶಮಂ ತು ವಿನಾಯಕಂ|<br />ಏಕಾದಶಂ ಗಣಪತಿಂ ದ್ವಾದಶಂ ತು ಗಜಾನನಂ|| ೪ ||</p><p class=\"has-text-align-center\">ದ್ವಾದಶೈತಾನಿ ನಾಮಾನಿ ತ್ರಿಸಂಧ್ಯಂ ಯಃ ಪಠೇನ್ನರಃ |<br />ನ ಚ ವಿಘ್ನಭಯಂ ತಸ್ಯ ಸರ್ವಸಿದ್ಧಿಕರಂ ಪ್ರಭೋ || ೫ ||</p><p class=\"has-text-align-center\">ವಿದ್ಯಾರ್ಥಿ ಲಭತೆ ವಿದ್ಯಾಂ ಧನಾರ್ಥೀ ಲಭತೆ ಧನಂ |<br />ಪುತ್ರಾರ್ಥಿ ಲಭತೆ ಪುತ್ರಾನ್ ಮೋಕ್ಷಾರ್ಥಿ ಲಭತೆ ಗತಿಂ|| ೬ ||</p><p class=\"has-text-align-center\">ಜಪೇತ್ ಗಣಪತಿಸ್ತೋತ್ರಂ ಷಡ್ಭಿರ್ಮಾಸೈಃ ಫಲಂ ಲಭೇತ್ |<br />ಸಂವತ್ಸರೇಣ ಸಿದ್ಧಿಂ ಚ ಲಭತೆ ನಾತ್ರ ಸಂಶಯಃ || ೭ ||</p><p class=\"has-text-align-center\">ಅಷ್ಟೆಭ್ಯೊ ಬ್ರಾಹ್ಮಣೇಭ್ಯಶ್ಚ ಲಿಖಿತ್ವಾ ಯಃ ಸಮರ್ಪಯೇತ್ |<br />ತಸ್ಯ ವಿದ್ಯಾ ಭವೇತ್ ಸರ್ವಾ ಗಣೇಶಸ್ಯ ಪ್ರಸಾದತಃ || ೮ ||</p><p class=\"has-text-align-center\">ಇತಿ ಶ್ರೀ ನಾರದ ಪುರಾಣೇ ಸಂಕಷ್ಟನಾಶನಂ ನಾಮ ಶ್ರೀ ಗಣಪತಿ ಸ್ತೋತ್ರಂ ಸಂಪೂರ್ಣಮ್.</p><h3><strong><span Kannada</a></span></strong></h3>"}},{"@type":"Question","name":"Ganesh Stotra Meaning with Lyrics in Sanskrit","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"<figure><p><img class=\"wp-image-1354 height=\"127\" /></p></figure><figure></figure><figure class=\"wp-block-image aligncenter size-full\"></figure><p>|| गणपति स्तोत्रम् ||</p><div class=\"panel-layout\"><div class=\"panel-grid panel-no-style\"><div class=\"panel-grid-cell\"><div class=\"so-panel widget widget_text panel-first-child panel-last-child\"><div class=\"panel-widget-style panel-widget-style-for-16-0-0-0\"><div class=\"textwidget\"><p>नारद उवाच </p><p>Narada Uvacha:</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">Sage Narada told</span></p><p>प्रणम्य शिरसा देवं गौरीपुत्रं विनायकम् ।।</p><p>भक्तावासं स्मरेन्नित्यमायु:कामार्थसिद्धये ।।१ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">The one seeking longevity, wealth, and love, Should bow their head in reverence To Lord Ganapathi, the son of Goddess Parvathi, Who is the embodiment of wisdom and grace ||1||</span></p><p>प्रथमं वक्रतुण्डं च एकदन्तं द्वितीयकम् ।।</p><p>तृतीयं कृष्णपिङ्गगाक्षं गजवक्त्रं चतुर्थकम् ।।२ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">First, perceive him as the deity with a broken tusk, Second, envision him as the Lord with a single tusk, Third, recognize him as the one with eyes of reddish-black hue, Fourth, behold him as the divine being with an elephant-like face.||2||</span></p><p>लम्बोदरं पञ्चमं च षष्ठं विकटमेव च ।।</p><p>सप्तमं विघ्नराजेन्द्रं धूम्रवर्णं तथाष्टमम् ।।३ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">Fifth, behold him with a broad and ample belly, Sixth, recognize him as the fierce adversary of his foes, Seventh, revere him as the remover of all obstacles, Eighth, perceive him with a complexion akin to the hue of smoke||3||</span></p><p>नवमं भालचन्द्रं च दशमं तु विनायकम् ।</p><p>एकादशं गणपतिं द्वादशं तु गजाननम् ।।४ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">Ninth, acknowledge him with the crescent adorning his forehead, Tenth, honor him as the supreme leader in removing obstacles, Eleventh, revere him as the commander of Lord Shiva's celestial army, And twelfth, behold him with the majestic countenance of an elephant ||4||</span></p><p>द्वादशैतानि नामानि त्रिसंध्यं य: पठेन्नर: ।</p><p>न च विघ्नभयं तस्य सर्वसिद्धिकरं प्रभो ।।५ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">Anyone who recites these twelve names, At dawn, noon, and dusk, Shall never fear defeat, And shall always attain their desired goals.||5||</span></p><p>विद्यार्थी लभते विद्यां धनार्थी लभते धनम् ।</p><p>पुत्रार्थी लभते पुत्रान् मोक्षार्थी लभते गतिम् ।।६ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">The seeker of knowledge shall attain wisdom, The seeker of wealth shall attain abundance, The one desiring a son shall be blessed with a child, And the one seeking salvation shall attain liberation.||6||</span></p><p>जपेत् गणपतिस्तोत्रं षड्भिर्मासै: फलं लभेत् ।</p><p>संवत्सरेण सिद्धिं च लभते नात्र संशय: ।।७ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">The fruits of chanting this prayer, To Lord Ganapati, shall manifest in six months, And within a year, all desires shall be fulfilled, With no doubt remaining, this truth stands affirmed.||7||</span></p><p>अष्टभ्यो ब्राह्मणेभ्यश्च लिखित्वा य: समर्पयेत् ।</p><p>तस्य विद्या भवेत्सर्वा गणेशस्य प्रसादत: ।।८ ।।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">The one who shares this prayer, In writing, with eight wise beings, And presents it as an offering to Lord Ganesha, Shall be bestowed with wisdom, And blessed with virtues by the grace of Lord Ganesha.||8||</span></p><p>इति श्री नारदपुराणे संकटविनाशनं श्रीगणपतिस्तोत्रं संपूर्णम् ।</p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\">Thus concludes the sacred prayer from the Narada Purana to Lord Ganesha, Which has the power to dispel all sorrows and afflictions.</span></p><p> </p></div></div></div></div></div></div>"}},{"@type":"Question","name":"Ganesh Stotra Meaning with Lyrics in English","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"<figure><p><img class=\"wp-image-1354 aligncenter\" src=\"http://ganeshastotram.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/cropped-cropped-siteiconimage-1-300x300.jpg\" alt=\"Ganpati stotra meaning in English with Sanskrit lyrics\" width=\"127\" height=\"127\" /></p></figure><figure></figure><figure class=\"wp-block-image aligncenter size-full\"></figure><div class=\"textwidget\"><p><strong>|| Ganapati Stotra || </strong></p><p><strong>Narada Uvacha:</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>Sage Narada told</strong></span></p><p><strong>Pranamya shirasa devam Gauri vinayakam Bhaktavasam smare nityam ayuh kamartha siddhaye ||1||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>The one seeking longevity, wealth, and love, Should bow their head in reverence To Lord Ganapathi, the son of Goddess Parvathi, Who is the embodiment of wisdom and grace ||1||</strong></span></p><p><strong>Prathamam vakratundam cha ekadantam dvitiyakam Tritiyam krishnapingaksham, gajavaktram chaturthakam ||2||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>First, perceive him as the deity with a broken tusk, Second, envision him as the Lord with a single tusk, Third, recognize him as the one with eyes of reddish-black hue, Fourth, behold him as the divine being with an elephant-like face.||2||</strong></span></p><p><strong>Lambodaram panchamam cha shashtam Vikatameva cha Saptamam Vighnarajendraṃ, Dhoomravarnam tathaashtamam ||3||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>Fifth, behold him with a broad and ample belly, Sixth, recognize him as the fierce adversary of his foes, Seventh, revere him as the remover of all obstacles, Eighth, perceive him with a complexion akin to the hue of smoke||3||</strong></span></p><p><strong>Navamam Bhalachandram cha dashamam tu Vinayakam Ekadasham ganapatim, dvadasham tu gajananam ||4||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>Ninth, acknowledge him with the crescent adorning his forehead, Tenth, honor him as the supreme leader in removing obstacles, Eleventh, revere him as the commander of Lord Shiva's celestial army, And twelfth, behold him with the majestic countenance of an elephant ||4||</strong></span></p><p><strong>Dvadashaitani namani trisandhyam yah pathen naraha Na cha vighna bhayam tasya sarvasiddhi karam prabho ||5||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>Anyone who recites these twelve names, At dawn, noon, and dusk, Shall never fear defeat, And shall always attain their desired goals.||5||</strong></span></p><p><strong>Vidyarthi labhate vidyam, dhanarthi labhate dhanam Putrarthi labhate putran, mo ksharthi labhate gatim ||6||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>The seeker of knowledge shall attain wisdom, The seeker of wealth shall attain abundance, The one desiring a son shall be blessed with a child, And the one seeking salvation shall attain liberation.||6||</strong></span></p><p><strong>Japed Ganapati Stotram shadbhir masaihi phalam labhet Samvatsaren Siddhim cha labhate natra sanshayah ||7||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>The fruits of chanting this prayer, To Lord Ganapati, shall manifest in six months, And within a year, all desires shall be fulfilled, With no doubt remaining, this truth stands affirmed.||7||</strong></span></p><p><strong>Ashtabhyo brahmanebhyashcha likhitva yah samarpayet Tasya vidya bhavet sarva ganeshasya prasadatah ||8||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>The one who shares this prayer, In writing, with eight wise beings, And presents it as an offering to Lord Ganesha, Shall be bestowed with wisdom, And blessed with virtues by the grace of Lord Ganesha.||8||</strong></span></p><p><strong> Iti Shri Narada Purane Sankshipta Nashana Nam Shri Ganapati Stotram Sampurnam ||</strong></p><p><span style=\"color: #800000\"><strong>Thus concludes the sacred prayer from the Narada Purana to Lord Ganesha, Which has the power to dispel all sorrows and afflictions.</strong></span></p></div>"}}]}</script>

					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
